In almost all cases,\n52:     // this is the right option to choose for this setting.\n53:     AUTO = 0;\n54: \n55:     // The connection manager will assume that the client is speaking HTTP/1.1.\n56:     HTTP1 = 1;\n57: \n58:     // The connection manager will assume that the client is speaking HTTP/2\n59:     // (Envoy does not require HTTP/2 to take place over TLS or to use ALPN.\n60:     // Prior knowledge is allowed).\n61:     HTTP2 = 2;\n62: \n63:     // The connection manager will assume that the client is speaking HTTP/3.\n64:     // This needs to be consistent with listener and transport socket config.\n65:     HTTP3 = 3;\n66:   }\n67: \n68:   enum ServerHeaderTransformation {\n69:     // Overwrite any Server header with the contents of server_name.\n70:     OVERWRITE = 0;\n71: \n72:     // If no Server header is present, append Server server_name\n73:     // If a Server header is present, pass it through.\n74:     APPEND_IF_ABSENT = 1;\n75: \n76:     // Pass through the value of the server header, and do not append a header\n77:     // if none is present.\n78:     PASS_THROUGH = 2;\n79:   }\n80: \n81:   // How to handle the :ref:`config_http_conn_man_headers_x-forwarded-client-cert` (XFCC) HTTP\n82:   // header.\n83:   enum ForwardClientCertDetails {\n84:     // Do not send the XFCC header to the next hop. This is the default value.\n85:     SANITIZE = 0;\n86: \n87:     // When the client connection is mTLS (Mutual TLS), forward the XFCC header\n88:     // in the request.\n89:     FORWARD_ONLY = 1;\n90: \n91:     // When the client connection is mTLS, append the client certificate\n92:     // information to the request’s XFCC header and forward it.\n93:     APPEND_FORWARD = 2;\n94: \n95:     // When the client connection is mTLS, reset the XFCC header with the client\n96:     // certificate information and send it to the next hop.\n97:     SANITIZE_SET = 3;\n98: \n99:     // Always forward the XFCC header in the request, regardless of whether the\n100:     // client connection is mTLS.\n101: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367@d9596a37e1620efc399ac5ce4821e268985e7dcc/-/blob/envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto%3FL1-100"}}}

involves a clear separation between configuration-time registration (in `HttpConnectionManagerConfig`) and runtime execution (in `FilterManager`).\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. FilterChainFactory Interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 89)\\nThe `FilterChainFactory` interface defines the contract for creating filter chains:\\n- **createFilterChain()** - Called when a new HTTP stream is created on the connection. It receives a `FilterChainManager` where it applies filter factories.\\n- **createUpgradeFilterChain()** - Creates special filter chains for HTTP upgrade scenarios (e.g., WebSocket).\\n- Located in `envoy/http/filter_factory.h`\\n\\n### 2. FilterChainManager Interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 70)\\nThe `FilterChainManager` is the \\\"sink\\\" where filter factories are applied:\\n- **applyFilterFactoryCb()** - Applies a filter factory callback with contextual information.\\n- Implemented by `FilterManager` for actual stream-level execution.\\n\\n### 3. FilterFactoryCb Function Type (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 24)\\nA `FilterFactoryCb` is a function that creates filters for a specific stream:\\n```cpp\\nusing FilterFactoryCb = std::function<void(FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks)>;\\n```\\nEach filter factory receives callbacks to add decoder/encoder filters to the chain.\\n\\n### 4. FilterChainHelper Template (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, line 69)\\nThe `FilterChainHelper` template processes HTTP filter configuration from protobuf:\\n- **processFilters()** - Iterates through HttpFilter proto configs and creates FilterFactoryCb for each.\\n- **processFilter()** - Processes a single HttpFilter config, looks up the registered factory, and creates a FilterFactoryCb.\\n- Handles static and dynamic filter configs.\\n- Validates filter dependencies.\\n- Used by `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` during initialization.\\n\\n### 5. FilterManager Implementation (source/common/http/filter_manager.h, line 638)\\nThe concrete `FilterManager` class executes filters at runtime:\\n- Inherits from `FilterChainManager` and `ScopeTrackedObject`.\\n- **applyFilterFactoryCb()** - Calls the factory callback to add filters to the stream.\\n- **decodeHeaders()** - Starts filter chain execution for request headers.\\n- **encodeHeaders()** - Starts filter chain execution for response headers.\\n- Maintains lists of decoder and encoder filters.\\n- Manages filter iteration and state tracking.\\n\\n### 6. HttpConnectionManagerConfig (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h, line 127)\\nThe main configuration class that implements `FilterChainFactory`:\\n- Processes HttpConnectionManager proto config during initialization.\\n- Stores `filter_factories_` - a list of `FilterFactoryCb` created by `FilterChainHelper`.\\n- **createFilterChain()** - Implementation at line 780-784 of config.cc:\\n  ```cpp\\n  bool HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain(Http::FilterChainManager& manager, bool,\\n                                                      const Http::FilterChainOptions& options) const {\\n    Http::FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories(manager, options, filter_factories_);\\n    return true;\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- Creates the filter chain by delegating to `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories`.\\n\\n### 7. FilterChainUtility (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h, line 42)\\nStatic utility methods for filter chain operations:\\n- **createFilterChainForFactories()** - Iterates through `FilterFactoriesList` and applies each factory callback to the manager, respecting filter disabled status and handling missing configs.\\n- Located in `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc`.\\n\\n### 8. HttpConnectionManager Proto (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, line 43)\\nProtobuf message defining HTTP connection manager configuration:\\n- **http_filters** field (line 471) - `repeated HttpFilter http_filters = 5;` - Defines the list of HTTP filters to be created for each stream.\\n- **upgrade_configs** field - Defines upgrade-specific filter chains.\\n- Other configuration fields like codec_type, stat_prefix, routing config, etc.\\n\\n### 9. HttpFilter Proto Message (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, line 1339)\\nProtobuf message defining a single HTTP filter:\\n- Contains filter name and typed configuration.\\n- Supports both static and dynamic (via config_discovery) configurations.\\n- Can be marked as disabled or optional.\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n### Registration Phase (Configuration Time)\\n1. **HttpConnectionManager Filter Network Filter** receives the HttpConnectionManager proto config.\\n2. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig constructor** processes the config:\\n   - Uses `FilterChainHelper<Server::Configuration::FactoryContext, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>` to process `config.http_filters()`.\\n   - `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()` iterates through each HttpFilter proto.\\n   - For each filter, `FilterChainHelper::processFilter()` looks up the registered factory using `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NeutralNamedHttpFilterFactory>`.\\n   - Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to create a `FilterFactoryCb`.\\n   - Stores these callbacks in a `FilterFactoriesList`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig stores** the list of `FilterFactoryCb` in `filter_factories_` member.\\n\\n### Execution Phase (Runtime)\\n1. **New HTTP stream arrives** at the connection (either from client or internally created).\\n2. **HttpConnectionManager** creates a new `FilterManager` and calls `filter_chain_factory_->createFilterChain(filter_manager_)`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()** is called:\\n   - Calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` with the stored `filter_factories_`.\\n4. **FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()** iterates through each `FilterFactoryCb`:\\n   - Checks if the filter is disabled (via route config or explicitly).\\n   - Calls the `FilterFactoryCb` function, passing the `FilterManager` as the `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks`.\\n   - Each callback adds decoder and/or encoder filters to the `FilterManager` using methods like `addStreamDecoderFilter()` and `addStreamEncoderFilter()`.\\n5. **FilterManager::decodeHeaders()** is called when request headers arrive:\\n   - Iterates through the decoder_filters_ list in order.\\n   - Calls each filter's `decodeHeaders()` method.\\n   - Continues until a filter stops iteration or all filters complete.\\n6. **Similar flow** for decode data, decode trailers, encode headers, encode data, and encode trailers.\\n7. **Filter execution** continues until the stream completes or terminates.\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Factory Pattern** - Factories create filters from proto configs, allowing flexible filter registration.\\n2. **Strategy Pattern** - Each filter implements the filter interface and can be swapped in/out.\\n3. **Chain of Responsibility** - Filters form a chain where each processes and potentially modifies data.\\n4. **Template Method** - `FilterChainHelper` uses templates to generalize filter processing for different contexts (downstream vs upstream).\\n5. **Separation of Concerns** - Configuration processing separated from runtime execution.\\n\\n## Configuration to Execution Mapping\\n\\n- **Proto Config** (HttpConnectionManager.http_filters) → **Factory Lookup** (Registry) → **FilterFactoryCb Creation** (factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto) → **Storage** (HttpConnectionManagerConfig.filter_factories_) → **Runtime Application** (FilterManager via applyFilterFactoryCb)\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2916,"cache_read_input_tokens":97305,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2916},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f03444ef-ba4d-4730-87be-72e9cad7e7ce","uuid":"f7dcdc8c-5e22-4f7f-8978-c87c2e680872"}

HttpFilter Proto Message (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, line 1339)\\nProtobuf message defining a single HTTP filter:\\n- Contains filter name and typed configuration.\\n- Supports both static and dynamic (via config_discovery) configurations.\\n- Can be marked as disabled or optional.\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n### Registration Phase (Configuration Time)\\n1. **HttpConnectionManager Filter Network Filter** receives the HttpConnectionManager proto config.\\n2. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig constructor** processes the config:\\n   - Uses `FilterChainHelper<Server::Configuration::FactoryContext, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>` to process `config.http_filters()`.\\n   - `FilterChainHelper::processFilters()` iterates through each HttpFilter proto.\\n   - For each filter, `FilterChainHelper::processFilter()` looks up the registered factory using `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NeutralNamedHttpFilterFactory>`.\\n   - Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to create a `FilterFactoryCb`.\\n   - Stores these callbacks in a `FilterFactoriesList`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig stores** the list of `FilterFactoryCb` in `filter_factories_` member.\\n\\n### Execution Phase (Runtime)\\n1. **New HTTP stream arrives** at the connection (either from client or internally created).\\n2. **HttpConnectionManager** creates a new `FilterManager` and calls `filter_chain_factory_->createFilterChain(filter_manager_)`.\\n3. **HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()** is called:\\n   - Calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` with the stored `filter_factories_`.\\n4. **FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()** iterates through each `FilterFactoryCb`:\\n   - Checks if the filter is disabled (via route config or explicitly).\\n   - Calls the `FilterFactoryCb` function, passing the `FilterManager` as the `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks`.\\n   - Each callback adds decoder and/or encoder filters to the `FilterManager` using methods like `addStreamDecoderFilter()` and `addStreamEncoderFilter()`.\\n5. **FilterManager::decodeHeaders()** is called when request headers arrive:\\n   - Iterates through the decoder_filters_ list in order.\\n   - Calls each filter's `decodeHeaders()` method.\\n   - Continues until a filter stops iteration or all filters complete.\\n6. **Similar flow** for decode data, decode trailers, encode headers, encode data, and encode trailers.\\n7. **Filter execution** continues until the stream completes or terminates.\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Factory Pattern** - Factories create filters from proto configs, allowing flexible filter registration.\\n2. **Strategy Pattern** - Each filter implements the filter interface and can be swapped in/out.\\n3. **Chain of Responsibility** - Filters form a chain where each processes and potentially modifies data.\\n4. **Template Method** - `FilterChainHelper` uses templates to generalize filter processing for different contexts (downstream vs upstream).\\n5. **Separation of Concerns** - Configuration processing separated from runtime execution.\\n\\n## Configuration to Execution Mapping\\n\\n- **Proto Config** (HttpConnectionManager.http_filters) → **Factory Lookup** (Registry) → **FilterFactoryCb Creation** (factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto) → **Storage** (HttpConnectionManagerConfig.filter_factories_) → **Runtime Application** (FilterManager via applyFilterFactoryCb)\\n\"\n   100→}\n   101→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. FilterChainFactory Interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h, line 89)\\nThe `FilterChainFactory` interface defines the contract for creating filter chains:\\n- **createFilterChain()** - Called when a new HTTP stream is created on the connection.
